\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+MANBRIEF\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+ graph management functions of the low-\/level CUDA driver API (\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+CURRENT\+\_\+\+FILE\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+) \+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+ENDMANBRIEF\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+

This section describes the graph management functions of the low-\/level CUDA driver application programming interface. 

\doxysubsection{Function Documentation}
\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a___g_r_a_p_h_ga3829323980ce7c3f272f481853d0a5fa}\label{group___c_u_d_a___g_r_a_p_h_ga3829323980ce7c3f272f481853d0a5fa}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuDeviceGetGraphMemAttribute()}{cuDeviceGetGraphMemAttribute()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Device\+Get\+Graph\+Mem\+Attribute (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga41ca2a24a242b36ef2ca77330b5fb72a}{CUdevice}}}]{device,  }\item[{CUgraph\+Mem\+\_\+attribute}]{attr,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{value }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Query asynchronous allocation attributes related to graphs. 

Valid attributes are\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CU\+\_\+\+GRAPH\+\_\+\+MEM\+\_\+\+ATTR\+\_\+\+USED\+\_\+\+MEM\+\_\+\+CURRENT\+:} Amount of memory, in bytes, currently associated with graphs
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CU\+\_\+\+GRAPH\+\_\+\+MEM\+\_\+\+ATTR\+\_\+\+USED\+\_\+\+MEM\+\_\+\+HIGH\+:} High watermark of memory, in bytes, associated with graphs since the last time it was reset. High watermark can only be reset to zero.
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CU\+\_\+\+GRAPH\+\_\+\+MEM\+\_\+\+ATTR\+\_\+\+RESERVED\+\_\+\+MEM\+\_\+\+CURRENT\+:} Amount of memory, in bytes, currently allocated for use by the CUDA graphs asynchronous allocator.
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CU\+\_\+\+GRAPH\+\_\+\+MEM\+\_\+\+ATTR\+\_\+\+RESERVED\+\_\+\+MEM\+\_\+\+HIGH\+:} High watermark of memory, in bytes, currently allocated for use by the CUDA graphs asynchronous allocator.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\index{Graph Management@{Graph Management}!cuDeviceGraphMemTrim@{cuDeviceGraphMemTrim}}
\index{cuDeviceGraphMemTrim@{cuDeviceGraphMemTrim}!Graph Management@{Graph Management}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuDeviceGraphMemTrim()}{cuDeviceGraphMemTrim()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Device\+Graph\+Mem\+Trim (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga41ca2a24a242b36ef2ca77330b5fb72a}{CUdevice}}}]{device }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Free unused memory that was cached on the specified device for use with graphs back to the OS. 

Blocks which are not in use by a graph that is either currently executing or scheduled to execute are freed back to the operating system.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em device} & -\/ The device for which cached memory should be freed.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Device\+Set\+Graph\+Mem\+Attribute (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga41ca2a24a242b36ef2ca77330b5fb72a}{CUdevice}}}]{device,  }\item[{CUgraph\+Mem\+\_\+attribute}]{attr,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{value }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Set asynchronous allocation attributes related to graphs. 

Valid attributes are\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CU\+\_\+\+GRAPH\+\_\+\+MEM\+\_\+\+ATTR\+\_\+\+USED\+\_\+\+MEM\+\_\+\+HIGH\+:} High watermark of memory, in bytes, associated with graphs since the last time it was reset. High watermark can only be reset to zero.
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CU\+\_\+\+GRAPH\+\_\+\+MEM\+\_\+\+ATTR\+\_\+\+RESERVED\+\_\+\+MEM\+\_\+\+HIGH\+:} High watermark of memory, in bytes, currently allocated for use by the CUDA graphs asynchronous allocator.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuGraphAddChildGraphNode()}{cuGraphAddChildGraphNode()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Graph\+Add\+Child\+Graph\+Node (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gac72514a94dacc85ed0617f979211079c}{CUgraph\+Node}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{ph\+Graph\+Node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga69f555c38df5b3fa1ed25efef794739a}{CUgraph}}}]{h\+Graph,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gac72514a94dacc85ed0617f979211079c}{CUgraph\+Node}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dependencies,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{num\+Dependencies,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga69f555c38df5b3fa1ed25efef794739a}{CUgraph}}}]{child\+Graph }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Creates a child graph node and adds it to a graph. 

Creates a new node which executes an embedded graph, and adds it to {\ttfamily h\+Graph} with {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} dependencies specified via {\ttfamily dependencies}. It is possible for {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} to be 0, in which case the node will be placed at the root of the graph. {\ttfamily dependencies} may not have any duplicate entries. A handle to the new node will be returned in {\ttfamily ph\+Graph\+Node}.

If {\ttfamily h\+Graph} contains allocation or free nodes, this call will return an error.

The node executes an embedded child graph. The child graph is cloned in this call.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ph\+Graph\+Node} & -\/ Returns newly created node \\
\hline
{\em h\+Graph} & -\/ Graph to which to add the node \\
\hline
{\em dependencies} & -\/ Dependencies of the node \\
\hline
{\em num\+Dependencies} & -\/ Number of dependencies \\
\hline
{\em child\+Graph} & -\/ The graph to clone into this node\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa0eed720f8a87cd1c5fd1c453bc7a03d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+SUCCESS}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaacf52f132faf29b473cdda6061f0f44a}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+DEINITIALIZED}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa8feb999f0af99b4a25ab26b3866f4df8}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa90696c86fcee1f536a1ec7d25867feeb}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE}, \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+graph\+\_\+thread\+\_\+safety \textbackslash{}notefnerr
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuGraphAddDependencies()}{cuGraphAddDependencies()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Graph\+Add\+Dependencies (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga69f555c38df5b3fa1ed25efef794739a}{CUgraph}}}]{h\+Graph,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gac72514a94dacc85ed0617f979211079c}{CUgraph\+Node}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{from,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gac72514a94dacc85ed0617f979211079c}{CUgraph\+Node}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{to,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{num\+Dependencies }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Adds dependency edges to a graph. 

The number of dependencies to be added is defined by {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} Elements in {\ttfamily from} and {\ttfamily to} at corresponding indices define a dependency. Each node in {\ttfamily from} and {\ttfamily to} must belong to {\ttfamily h\+Graph}.

If {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} is 0, elements in {\ttfamily from} and {\ttfamily to} will be ignored. Specifying an existing dependency will return an error.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em h\+Graph} & -\/ Graph to which dependencies are added \\
\hline
{\em from} & -\/ Array of nodes that provide the dependencies \\
\hline
{\em to} & -\/ Array of dependent nodes \\
\hline
{\em num\+Dependencies} & -\/ Number of dependencies to be added\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuGraphAddEmptyNode()}{cuGraphAddEmptyNode()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Graph\+Add\+Empty\+Node (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gac72514a94dacc85ed0617f979211079c}{CUgraph\+Node}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{ph\+Graph\+Node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga69f555c38df5b3fa1ed25efef794739a}{CUgraph}}}]{h\+Graph,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gac72514a94dacc85ed0617f979211079c}{CUgraph\+Node}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dependencies,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{num\+Dependencies }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Creates an empty node and adds it to a graph. 

Creates a new node which performs no operation, and adds it to {\ttfamily h\+Graph} with {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} dependencies specified via {\ttfamily dependencies}. It is possible for {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} to be 0, in which case the node will be placed at the root of the graph. {\ttfamily dependencies} may not have any duplicate entries. A handle to the new node will be returned in {\ttfamily ph\+Graph\+Node}.

An empty node performs no operation during execution, but can be used for transitive ordering. For example, a phased execution graph with 2 groups of n nodes with a barrier between them can be represented using an empty node and 2\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}n dependency edges, rather than no empty node and n\texorpdfstring{$^\wedge$}{\string^}2 dependency edges.

{\em h\+Graph} & -\/ Graph to which to add the node \\
\hline
{\em dependencies} & -\/ Dependencies of the node \\
\hline
{\em num\+Dependencies} & -\/ Number of dependencies\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Graph\+Add\+Event\+Record\+Node (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gac72514a94dacc85ed0617f979211079c}{CUgraph\+Node}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{ph\+Graph\+Node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga69f555c38df5b3fa1ed25efef794739a}{CUgraph}}}]{h\+Graph,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gac72514a94dacc85ed0617f979211079c}{CUgraph\+Node}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dependencies,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{num\+Dependencies,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga6d740185cf0953636d4ae37f68d7559b}{CUevent}}}]{event }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Creates an event record node and adds it to a graph. 

Creates a new event record node and adds it to {\ttfamily h\+Graph} with {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} dependencies specified via {\ttfamily dependencies} and event specified in {\ttfamily event}. It is possible for {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} to be 0, in which case the node will be placed at the root of the graph. {\ttfamily dependencies} may not have any duplicate entries. A handle to the new node will be returned in {\ttfamily ph\+Graph\+Node}.

Each launch of the graph will record {\ttfamily event} to capture execution of the node\textquotesingle{}s dependencies.

{\em dependencies} & -\/ Dependencies of the node \\
\hline
{\em num\+Dependencies} & -\/ Number of dependencies \\
\hline
{\em event} & -\/ Event for the node\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuGraphAddEventWaitNode()}{cuGraphAddEventWaitNode()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Graph\+Add\+Event\+Wait\+Node (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gac72514a94dacc85ed0617f979211079c}{CUgraph\+Node}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{ph\+Graph\+Node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga69f555c38df5b3fa1ed25efef794739a}{CUgraph}}}]{h\+Graph,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gac72514a94dacc85ed0617f979211079c}{CUgraph\+Node}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dependencies,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{num\+Dependencies,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga6d740185cf0953636d4ae37f68d7559b}{CUevent}}}]{event }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Creates an event wait node and adds it to a graph. 

Creates a new event wait node and adds it to {\ttfamily h\+Graph} with {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} dependencies specified via {\ttfamily dependencies} and event specified in {\ttfamily event}. It is possible for {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} to be 0, in which case the node will be placed at the root of the graph. {\ttfamily dependencies} may not have any duplicate entries. A handle to the new node will be returned in {\ttfamily ph\+Graph\+Node}.

The graph node will wait for all work captured in {\ttfamily event}. See \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___e_v_e_n_t_ga8b5c6177fdc919e456a73684a01d2bac}{cu\+Event\+Record()} for details on what is captured by an event. {\ttfamily event} may be from a different context or device than the launch stream.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ph\+Graph\+Node} & -\/ Returns newly created node \\
\hline
{\em h\+Graph} & -\/ Graph to which to add the node \\
\hline
{\em dependencies} & -\/ Dependencies of the node \\
\hline
{\em num\+Dependencies} & -\/ Number of dependencies \\
\hline
{\em event} & -\/ Event for the node\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Graph\+Add\+External\+Semaphores\+Signal\+Node (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gac72514a94dacc85ed0617f979211079c}{CUgraph\+Node}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{ph\+Graph\+Node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga69f555c38df5b3fa1ed25efef794739a}{CUgraph}}}]{h\+Graph,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gac72514a94dacc85ed0617f979211079c}{CUgraph\+Node}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dependencies,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{num\+Dependencies,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_c_u_d_a___e_x_t___s_e_m___s_i_g_n_a_l___n_o_d_e___p_a_r_a_m_s__st}{CUDA\+\_\+\+EXT\+\_\+\+SEM\+\_\+\+SIGNAL\+\_\+\+NODE\+\_\+\+PARAMS}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{node\+Params }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Creates an external semaphore signal node and adds it to a graph. 

Creates a new external semaphore signal node and adds it to {\ttfamily h\+Graph} with {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} dependencies specified via {\ttfamily dependencies} and arguments specified in {\ttfamily node\+Params}. It is possible for {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} to be 0, in which case the node will be placed at the root of the graph. {\ttfamily dependencies} may not have any duplicate entries. A handle to the new node will be returned in {\ttfamily ph\+Graph\+Node}.

Performs a signal operation on a set of externally allocated semaphore objects when the node is launched. The operation(s) will occur after all of the node\textquotesingle{}s dependencies have completed.

It is possible for {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} to be 0, in which case the node will be placed at the root of the graph. {\ttfamily dependencies} may not have any duplicate entries. {\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Graph\+Add\+Host\+Node (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gac72514a94dacc85ed0617f979211079c}{CUgraph\+Node}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{ph\+Graph\+Node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga69f555c38df5b3fa1ed25efef794739a}{CUgraph}}}]{h\+Graph,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gac72514a94dacc85ed0617f979211079c}{CUgraph\+Node}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dependencies,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{num\+Dependencies,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_c_u_d_a___h_o_s_t___n_o_d_e___p_a_r_a_m_s__st}{CUDA\+\_\+\+HOST\+\_\+\+NODE\+\_\+\+PARAMS}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{node\+Params }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Creates a host execution node and adds it to a graph. 

Creates a new CPU execution node and adds it to {\ttfamily h\+Graph} with {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} dependencies specified via {\ttfamily dependencies} and arguments specified in {\ttfamily node\+Params}. It is possible for {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} to be 0, in which case the node will be placed at the root of the graph. {\ttfamily dependencies} may not have any duplicate entries. A handle to the new node will be returned in {\ttfamily ph\+Graph\+Node}.

When the graph is launched, the node will invoke the specified CPU function. Host nodes are not supported under MPS with pre-\/\+Volta GPUs.

\hline

\hline
{\em num\+Dependencies} & -\/ Number of dependencies \\
\hline
{\em node\+Params} & -\/ Parameters for the host node\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{cuGraphAddKernelNode@{cuGraphAddKernelNode}!Graph Management@{Graph Management}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuGraphAddKernelNode()}{cuGraphAddKernelNode()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Graph\+Add\+Kernel\+Node (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gac72514a94dacc85ed0617f979211079c}{CUgraph\+Node}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{ph\+Graph\+Node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga69f555c38df5b3fa1ed25efef794739a}{CUgraph}}}]{h\+Graph,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gac72514a94dacc85ed0617f979211079c}{CUgraph\+Node}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dependencies,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{num\+Dependencies,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_c_u_d_a___k_e_r_n_e_l___n_o_d_e___p_a_r_a_m_s__st}{CUDA\+\_\+\+KERNEL\+\_\+\+NODE\+\_\+\+PARAMS}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{node\+Params }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Creates a kernel execution node and adds it to a graph. 

Creates a new kernel execution node and adds it to {\ttfamily h\+Graph} with {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} dependencies specified via {\ttfamily dependencies} and arguments specified in {\ttfamily node\+Params}. It is possible for {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} to be 0, in which case the node will be placed at the root of the graph. {\ttfamily dependencies} may not have any duplicate entries. A handle to the new node will be returned in {\ttfamily ph\+Graph\+Node}.

The CUDA\+\_\+\+KERNEL\+\_\+\+NODE\+\_\+\+PARAMS structure is defined as\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{typedef}\ \textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_c_u_d_a___k_e_r_n_e_l___n_o_d_e___p_a_r_a_m_s__st}{CUDA\_KERNEL\_NODE\_PARAMS\_st}}\ \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned}\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_c_u_d_a___k_e_r_n_e_l___n_o_d_e___p_a_r_a_m_s__st_a28de5d6a977ae0f368cbd921a6725932}{blockDimX}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned}\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_c_u_d_a___k_e_r_n_e_l___n_o_d_e___p_a_r_a_m_s__st_a57c76f779a482146d8e8e63b21091f6e}{blockDimY}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned}\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_c_u_d_a___k_e_r_n_e_l___n_o_d_e___p_a_r_a_m_s__st_abb74a432d9b541b0ae3c2c0a25f27717}{blockDimZ}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned}\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_c_u_d_a___k_e_r_n_e_l___n_o_d_e___p_a_r_a_m_s__st_ad554f814ccf1527d10f6786998b30cd7}{sharedMemBytes}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ **\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_c_u_d_a___k_e_r_n_e_l___n_o_d_e___p_a_r_a_m_s__st_a1632f92f673db084993121218ad12649}{kernelParams}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ **\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_c_u_d_a___k_e_r_n_e_l___n_o_d_e___p_a_r_a_m_s__st_a2faf3979f682b7ca3d834e8c010ce0f5}{extra}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_c_u_d_a___k_e_r_n_e_l___n_o_d_e___p_a_r_a_m_s__st}{CUDA\_KERNEL\_NODE\_PARAMS}};}

\end{DoxyCode}


When the graph is launched, the node will invoke kernel {\ttfamily func} on a ({\ttfamily grid\+DimX} x {\ttfamily grid\+DimY} x {\ttfamily grid\+DimZ}) grid of blocks. Each block contains ({\ttfamily block\+DimX} x {\ttfamily block\+DimY} x {\ttfamily block\+DimZ}) threads.

{\ttfamily shared\+Mem\+Bytes} sets the amount of dynamic shared memory that will be available to each thread block.

Kernel parameters to {\ttfamily func} can be specified in one of two ways\+:

1) Kernel parameters can be specified via {\ttfamily kernel\+Params}. If the kernel has N parameters, then {\ttfamily kernel\+Params} needs to be an array of N pointers. Each pointer, from {\ttfamily kernel\+Params}\mbox{[}0\mbox{]} to {\ttfamily kernel\+Params}\mbox{[}N-\/1\mbox{]}, points to the region of memory from which the actual parameter will be copied. The number of kernel parameters and their offsets and sizes do not need to be specified as that information is retrieved directly from the kernel\textquotesingle{}s image.

2) Kernel parameters for non-\/cooperative kernels can also be packaged by the application into a single buffer that is passed in via {\ttfamily extra}. This places the burden on the application of knowing each kernel parameter\textquotesingle{}s size and alignment/padding within the buffer. The {\ttfamily extra} parameter exists to allow this function to take additional less commonly used arguments. {\ttfamily extra} specifies a list of names of extra settings and their corresponding values. Each extra setting name is immediately followed by the corresponding value. The list must be terminated with either NULL or CU\+\_\+\+LAUNCH\+\_\+\+PARAM\+\_\+\+END.


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gad5c11cff5adfa5a69d66829399653532}{CU\+\_\+\+LAUNCH\+\_\+\+PARAM\+\_\+\+END}, which indicates the end of the {\ttfamily extra} array;
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga36d10d0b40c51372877578a2cffd6acd}{CU\+\_\+\+LAUNCH\+\_\+\+PARAM\+\_\+\+BUFFER\+\_\+\+POINTER}, which specifies that the next value in {\ttfamily extra} will be a pointer to a buffer containing all the kernel parameters for launching kernel {\ttfamily func};
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf339c057cd94562ead93a192e11c17e9}{CU\+\_\+\+LAUNCH\+\_\+\+PARAM\+\_\+\+BUFFER\+\_\+\+SIZE}, which specifies that the next value in {\ttfamily extra} will be a pointer to a size\+\_\+t containing the size of the buffer specified with \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga36d10d0b40c51372877578a2cffd6acd}{CU\+\_\+\+LAUNCH\+\_\+\+PARAM\+\_\+\+BUFFER\+\_\+\+POINTER};
\end{DoxyItemize}

The error \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa90696c86fcee1f536a1ec7d25867feeb}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE} will be returned if kernel parameters are specified with both {\ttfamily kernel\+Params} and {\ttfamily extra} (i.\+e. both {\ttfamily kernel\+Params} and {\ttfamily extra} are non-\/\+NULL). \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa90696c86fcee1f536a1ec7d25867feeb}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE} will be returned if {\ttfamily extra} is used for a cooperative kernel.

The {\ttfamily kernel\+Params} or {\ttfamily extra} array, as well as the argument values it points to, are copied during this call.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Kernels launched using graphs must not use texture and surface references. Reading or writing through any texture or surface reference is undefined behavior. This restriction does not apply to texture and surface objects.
\end{DoxyNote}

\index{cuGraphAddMemAllocNode@{cuGraphAddMemAllocNode}!Graph Management@{Graph Management}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuGraphAddMemAllocNode()}{cuGraphAddMemAllocNode()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Graph\+Add\+Mem\+Alloc\+Node (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gac72514a94dacc85ed0617f979211079c}{CUgraph\+Node}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{ph\+Graph\+Node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga69f555c38df5b3fa1ed25efef794739a}{CUgraph}}}]{h\+Graph,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gac72514a94dacc85ed0617f979211079c}{CUgraph\+Node}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dependencies,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{num\+Dependencies,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gac27ce5ce8b444b2120a2a27712d93681}{CUDA\+\_\+\+MEM\+\_\+\+ALLOC\+\_\+\+NODE\+\_\+\+PARAMS}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{node\+Params }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Creates an allocation node and adds it to a graph. 

Creates a new allocation node and adds it to {\ttfamily h\+Graph} with {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} dependencies specified via {\ttfamily dependencies} and arguments specified in {\ttfamily node\+Params}. It is possible for {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} to be 0, in which case the node will be placed at the root of the graph. {\ttfamily dependencies} may not have any duplicate entries. A handle to the new node will be returned in {\ttfamily ph\+Graph\+Node}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ph\+Graph\+Node} & -\/ Returns newly created node \\
\hline
{\em h\+Graph} & -\/ Graph to which to add the node \\
\hline
{\em dependencies} & -\/ Dependencies of the node \\
\hline
{\em num\+Dependencies} & -\/ Number of dependencies \\
\hline
{\em node\+Params} & -\/ Parameters for the node\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
When \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___g_r_a_p_h_ga17f19579112ac9a7fef01d5f58985248}{cu\+Graph\+Add\+Mem\+Alloc\+Node} creates an allocation node, it returns the address of the allocation in {\ttfamily node\+Params.\+dptr}. The allocation\textquotesingle{}s address remains fixed across instantiations and launches.

If the allocation is freed in the same graph, by creating a free node using \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___g_r_a_p_h_ga21296523ef5537b27f98a1c56b2c264f}{cu\+Graph\+Add\+Mem\+Free\+Node}, the allocation can be accessed by nodes ordered after the allocation node but before the free node. These allocations cannot be freed outside the owning graph, and they can only be freed once in the owning graph.

If the allocation is not freed in the same graph, then it can be accessed not only by nodes in the graph which are ordered after the allocation node, but also by stream operations ordered after the graph\textquotesingle{}s execution but before the allocation is freed.

Allocations which are not freed in the same graph can be freed by\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item passing the allocation to \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___m_a_l_l_o_c___a_s_y_n_c_ga1e04649f84f307d199f7976854c89a45}{cu\+Mem\+Free\+Async} or cu\+Mem\+Free;
\item launching a graph with a free node for that allocation; or
\item specifying \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggac3b9348f257350775565dd26cc4ce6e3a1684f715bf05e39afd69aa508299a479}{CUDA\+\_\+\+GRAPH\+\_\+\+INSTANTIATE\+\_\+\+FLAG\+\_\+\+AUTO\+\_\+\+FREE\+\_\+\+ON\+\_\+\+LAUNCH} during instantiation, which makes each launch behave as though it called \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___m_a_l_l_o_c___a_s_y_n_c_ga1e04649f84f307d199f7976854c89a45}{cu\+Mem\+Free\+Async} for every unfreed allocation.
\end{DoxyItemize}

It is not possible to free an allocation in both the owning graph and another graph. If the allocation is freed in the same graph, a free node cannot be added to another graph. If the allocation is freed in another graph, a free node can no longer be added to the owning graph.

The following restrictions apply to graphs which contain allocation and/or memory free nodes\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Nodes and edges of the graph cannot be deleted.
\item The graph cannot be used in a child node.
\item Only one instantiation of the graph may exist at any point in time.
\item The graph cannot be cloned.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuGraphAddMemcpyNode()}{cuGraphAddMemcpyNode()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Graph\+Add\+Memcpy\+Node (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gac72514a94dacc85ed0617f979211079c}{CUgraph\+Node}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{ph\+Graph\+Node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga69f555c38df5b3fa1ed25efef794739a}{CUgraph}}}]{h\+Graph,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gac72514a94dacc85ed0617f979211079c}{CUgraph\+Node}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dependencies,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{num\+Dependencies,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_c_u_d_a___m_e_m_c_p_y3_d__st}{CUDA\+\_\+\+MEMCPY3D}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{copy\+Params,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf9f5bd81658f866613785b3a0bb7d7d9}{CUcontext}}}]{ctx }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Creates a memcpy node and adds it to a graph. 

Creates a new memcpy node and adds it to {\ttfamily h\+Graph} with {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} dependencies specified via {\ttfamily dependencies}. It is possible for {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} to be 0, in which case the node will be placed at the root of the graph. {\ttfamily dependencies} may not have any duplicate entries. A handle to the new node will be returned in {\ttfamily ph\+Graph\+Node}.

When the graph is launched, the node will perform the memcpy described by {\ttfamily copy\+Params}. See cu\+Memcpy3\+D() for a description of the structure and its restrictions.

Memcpy nodes have some additional restrictions with regards to managed memory, if the system contains at least one device which has a zero value for the device attribute \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga3b9f561d2a42733dde99b2cedcaa413aa33110e44c9cb6ead02f03ff6f6fd495e}{CU\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+ATTRIBUTE\+\_\+\+CONCURRENT\+\_\+\+MANAGED\+\_\+\+ACCESS}. If one or more of the operands refer to managed memory, then using the memory type \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga401176319b8c53648d525e8859437790a7a47ca2de6db5cf82084ad80ce66aa71}{CU\+\_\+\+MEMORYTYPE\+\_\+\+UNIFIED} is disallowed for those operand(s). The managed memory will be treated as residing on either the host or the device, depending on which memory type is specified.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ph\+Graph\+Node} & -\/ Returns newly created node \\
\hline
{\em h\+Graph} & -\/ Graph to which to add the node \\
\hline
{\em dependencies} & -\/ Dependencies of the node \\
\hline
{\em num\+Dependencies} & -\/ Number of dependencies \\
\hline
{\em copy\+Params} & -\/ Parameters for the memory copy \\
\hline
{\em ctx} & -\/ Context on which to run the node\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa0eed720f8a87cd1c5fd1c453bc7a03d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+SUCCESS}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaacf52f132faf29b473cdda6061f0f44a}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+DEINITIALIZED}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa8feb999f0af99b4a25ab26b3866f4df8}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa90696c86fcee1f536a1ec7d25867feeb}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE} \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+graph\+\_\+thread\+\_\+safety \textbackslash{}notefnerr
\end{DoxyReturn}

\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a___g_r_a_p_h_ga21296523ef5537b27f98a1c56b2c264f}\label{group___c_u_d_a___g_r_a_p_h_ga21296523ef5537b27f98a1c56b2c264f}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuGraphAddMemFreeNode()}{cuGraphAddMemFreeNode()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Graph\+Add\+Mem\+Free\+Node (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gac72514a94dacc85ed0617f979211079c}{CUgraph\+Node}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{ph\+Graph\+Node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga69f555c38df5b3fa1ed25efef794739a}{CUgraph}}}]{h\+Graph,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gac72514a94dacc85ed0617f979211079c}{CUgraph\+Node}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dependencies,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{num\+Dependencies,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga183f7b0d8ad008ea2a5fd552537ace4e}{CUdeviceptr}}}]{dptr }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Creates a memory free node and adds it to a graph. 

Creates a new memory free node and adds it to {\ttfamily h\+Graph} with {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} dependencies specified via {\ttfamily dependencies} and arguments specified in {\ttfamily node\+Params}. It is possible for {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} to be 0, in which case the node will be placed at the root of the graph. {\ttfamily dependencies} may not have any duplicate entries. A handle to the new node will be returned in {\ttfamily ph\+Graph\+Node}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ph\+Graph\+Node} & -\/ Returns newly created node \\
\hline
{\em h\+Graph} & -\/ Graph to which to add the node \\
\hline
{\em dependencies} & -\/ Dependencies of the node \\
\hline
{\em num\+Dependencies} & -\/ Number of dependencies \\
\hline
{\em dptr} & -\/ Address of memory to free\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___g_r_a_p_h_ga21296523ef5537b27f98a1c56b2c264f}{cu\+Graph\+Add\+Mem\+Free\+Node} will return \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa90696c86fcee1f536a1ec7d25867feeb}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE} if the user attempts to free\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item an allocation twice in the same graph.
\item an address that was not returned by an allocation node.
\item an invalid address.
\end{DoxyItemize}

The following restrictions apply to graphs which contain allocation and/or memory free nodes\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Nodes and edges of the graph cannot be deleted.
\item The graph cannot be used in a child node.
\item Only one instantiation of the graph may exist at any point in time.
\item The graph cannot be cloned.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa0eed720f8a87cd1c5fd1c453bc7a03d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+SUCCESS}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaacf52f132faf29b473cdda6061f0f44a}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+DEINITIALIZED}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa8feb999f0af99b4a25ab26b3866f4df8}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa54756ae7ade0dfd09faeccb513dd831b}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+SUPPORTED}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa90696c86fcee1f536a1ec7d25867feeb}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE} \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+graph\+\_\+thread\+\_\+safety \textbackslash{}notefnerr
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuGraphAddMemsetNode()}{cuGraphAddMemsetNode()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Graph\+Add\+Memset\+Node (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gac72514a94dacc85ed0617f979211079c}{CUgraph\+Node}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{ph\+Graph\+Node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga69f555c38df5b3fa1ed25efef794739a}{CUgraph}}}]{h\+Graph,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gac72514a94dacc85ed0617f979211079c}{CUgraph\+Node}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dependencies,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{num\+Dependencies,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_c_u_d_a___m_e_m_s_e_t___n_o_d_e___p_a_r_a_m_s__st}{CUDA\+\_\+\+MEMSET\+\_\+\+NODE\+\_\+\+PARAMS}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{memset\+Params,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf9f5bd81658f866613785b3a0bb7d7d9}{CUcontext}}}]{ctx }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Creates a memset node and adds it to a graph. 

Creates a new memset node and adds it to {\ttfamily h\+Graph} with {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} dependencies specified via {\ttfamily dependencies}. It is possible for {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} to be 0, in which case the node will be placed at the root of the graph. {\ttfamily dependencies} may not have any duplicate entries. A handle to the new node will be returned in {\ttfamily ph\+Graph\+Node}.

The element size must be 1, 2, or 4 bytes. When the graph is launched, the node will perform the memset described by {\ttfamily memset\+Params}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ph\+Graph\+Node} & -\/ Returns newly created node \\
\hline
{\em h\+Graph} & -\/ Graph to which to add the node \\
\hline
{\em dependencies} & -\/ Dependencies of the node \\
\hline
{\em num\+Dependencies} & -\/ Number of dependencies \\
\hline
{\em memset\+Params} & -\/ Parameters for the memory set \\
\hline
{\em ctx} & -\/ Context on which to run the node\\
\hline

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuGraphChildGraphNodeGetGraph()}{cuGraphChildGraphNodeGetGraph()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Graph\+Child\+Graph\+Node\+Get\+Graph (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gac72514a94dacc85ed0617f979211079c}{CUgraph\+Node}}}]{h\+Node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga69f555c38df5b3fa1ed25efef794739a}{CUgraph}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{ph\+Graph }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Gets a handle to the embedded graph of a child graph node. 

Gets a handle to the embedded graph in a child graph node. This call does not clone the graph. Changes to the graph will be reflected in the node, and the node retains ownership of the graph.

Allocation and free nodes cannot be added to the returned graph. Attempting to do so will return an error.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em h\+Node} & -\/ Node to get the embedded graph for \\
\hline
{\em ph\+Graph} & -\/ Location to store a handle to the graph\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Graph\+Clone (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga69f555c38df5b3fa1ed25efef794739a}{CUgraph}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{ph\+Graph\+Clone,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga69f555c38df5b3fa1ed25efef794739a}{CUgraph}}}]{original\+Graph }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Clones a graph. 

This function creates a copy of {\ttfamily original\+Graph} and returns it in {\ttfamily ph\+Graph\+Clone}. All parameters are copied into the cloned graph. The original graph may be modified after this call without affecting the clone.

Child graph nodes in the original graph are recursively copied into the clone.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ph\+Graph\+Clone} & -\/ Returns newly created cloned graph \\
\hline
{\em original\+Graph} & -\/ Graph to clone\\

\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Graph\+Debug\+Dot\+Print (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga69f555c38df5b3fa1ed25efef794739a}{CUgraph}}}]{h\+Graph,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{char}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{path,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{unsigned}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{int}}}]{flags }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Write a DOT file describing graph structure. 

Using the provided {\ttfamily h\+Graph}, write to {\ttfamily path} a DOT formatted description of the graph. By default this includes the graph topology, node types, node id, kernel names and memcpy direction. {\ttfamily flags} can be specified to write more detailed information about each node type such as parameter values, kernel attributes, node and function handles.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em h\+Graph} & -\/ The graph to create a DOT file from \\
\hline
{\em path} & -\/ The path to write the DOT file to \\
\hline
{\em flags} & -\/ Flags from CUgraph\+Debug\+Dot\+\_\+flags for specifying which additional node information to write\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Graph\+Destroy\+Node (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gac72514a94dacc85ed0617f979211079c}{CUgraph\+Node}}}]{h\+Node }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Remove a node from the graph. 

Removes {\ttfamily h\+Node} from its graph. This operation also severs any dependencies of other nodes on {\ttfamily h\+Node} and vice versa.

Nodes which belong to a graph which contains allocation or free nodes cannot be destroyed. Any attempt to do so will return an error.

\index{Graph Management@{Graph Management}!cuGraphExecChildGraphNodeSetParams@{cuGraphExecChildGraphNodeSetParams}}
\index{cuGraphExecChildGraphNodeSetParams@{cuGraphExecChildGraphNodeSetParams}!Graph Management@{Graph Management}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuGraphExecChildGraphNodeSetParams()}{cuGraphExecChildGraphNodeSetParams()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Graph\+Exec\+Child\+Graph\+Node\+Set\+Params (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf0abeceeaa9f0a39592fe36a538ea1f0}{CUgraph\+Exec}}}]{h\+Graph\+Exec,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gac72514a94dacc85ed0617f979211079c}{CUgraph\+Node}}}]{h\+Node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga69f555c38df5b3fa1ed25efef794739a}{CUgraph}}}]{child\+Graph }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Updates node parameters in the child graph node in the given graph\+Exec. 

Updates the work represented by {\ttfamily h\+Node} in {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec} as though the nodes contained in {\ttfamily h\+Node\textquotesingle{}s} graph had the parameters contained in {\ttfamily child\+Graph\textquotesingle{}s} nodes at instantiation. {\ttfamily h\+Node} must remain in the graph which was used to instantiate {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec}. Changed edges to and from {\ttfamily h\+Node} are ignored.

The modifications only affect future launches of {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec}. Already enqueued or running launches of {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec} are not affected by this call. {\ttfamily h\+Node} is also not modified by this call.

The topology of {\ttfamily child\+Graph}, as well as the node insertion order, must match that of the graph contained in {\ttfamily h\+Node}. See \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___g_r_a_p_h_gaeea2f038a4e76e7949b7c43c51848106}{cu\+Graph\+Exec\+Update()} for a list of restrictions on what can be updated in an instantiated graph. The update is recursive, so child graph nodes contained within the top level child graph will also be updated.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em h\+Graph\+Exec} & -\/ The executable graph in which to set the specified node \\
\hline
{\em h\+Node} & -\/ Host node from the graph which was used to instantiate graph\+Exec \\
\hline
{\em child\+Graph} & -\/ The graph supplying the updated parameters\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa0eed720f8a87cd1c5fd1c453bc7a03d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+SUCCESS}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa90696c86fcee1f536a1ec7d25867feeb}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE}, \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+graph\+\_\+thread\+\_\+safety \textbackslash{}notefnerr
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Graph\+Exec\+Destroy (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf0abeceeaa9f0a39592fe36a538ea1f0}{CUgraph\+Exec}}}]{h\+Graph\+Exec }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Destroys an executable graph. 

Destroys the executable graph specified by {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec}, as well as all of its executable nodes. If the executable graph is in-\/flight, it will not be terminated, but rather freed asynchronously on completion.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuGraphExecEventRecordNodeSetEvent()}{cuGraphExecEventRecordNodeSetEvent()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Graph\+Exec\+Event\+Record\+Node\+Set\+Event (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf0abeceeaa9f0a39592fe36a538ea1f0}{CUgraph\+Exec}}}]{h\+Graph\+Exec,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gac72514a94dacc85ed0617f979211079c}{CUgraph\+Node}}}]{h\+Node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga6d740185cf0953636d4ae37f68d7559b}{CUevent}}}]{event }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Sets the event for an event record node in the given graph\+Exec. 

Sets the event of an event record node in an executable graph {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec}. The node is identified by the corresponding node {\ttfamily h\+Node} in the non-\/executable graph, from which the executable graph was instantiated.

The modifications only affect future launches of {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec}. Already enqueued or running launches of {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec} are not affected by this call. {\ttfamily h\+Node} is also not modified by this call.

\hline
{\em h\+Node} & -\/ event record node from the graph from which graph\+Exec was instantiated \\
\hline

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuGraphExecEventWaitNodeSetEvent()}{cuGraphExecEventWaitNodeSetEvent()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Graph\+Exec\+Event\+Wait\+Node\+Set\+Event (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf0abeceeaa9f0a39592fe36a538ea1f0}{CUgraph\+Exec}}}]{h\+Graph\+Exec,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gac72514a94dacc85ed0617f979211079c}{CUgraph\+Node}}}]{h\+Node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga6d740185cf0953636d4ae37f68d7559b}{CUevent}}}]{event }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Sets the event for an event wait node in the given graph\+Exec. 

Sets the event of an event wait node in an executable graph {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec}. The node is identified by the corresponding node {\ttfamily h\+Node} in the non-\/executable graph, from which the executable graph was instantiated.

The modifications only affect future launches of {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec}. Already enqueued or running launches of {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec} are not affected by this call. {\ttfamily h\+Node} is also not modified by this call.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em h\+Graph\+Exec} & -\/ The executable graph in which to set the specified node \\
\hline
{\em h\+Node} & -\/ event wait node from the graph from which graph\+Exec was instantiated \\
\hline
{\em event} & -\/ Updated event to use\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Graph\+Exec\+External\+Semaphores\+Signal\+Node\+Set\+Params (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf0abeceeaa9f0a39592fe36a538ea1f0}{CUgraph\+Exec}}}]{h\+Graph\+Exec,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gac72514a94dacc85ed0617f979211079c}{CUgraph\+Node}}}]{h\+Node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_c_u_d_a___e_x_t___s_e_m___s_i_g_n_a_l___n_o_d_e___p_a_r_a_m_s__st}{CUDA\+\_\+\+EXT\+\_\+\+SEM\+\_\+\+SIGNAL\+\_\+\+NODE\+\_\+\+PARAMS}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{node\+Params }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Sets the parameters for an external semaphore signal node in the given graph\+Exec. 

Sets the parameters of an external semaphore signal node in an executable graph {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec}. The node is identified by the corresponding node {\ttfamily h\+Node} in the non-\/executable graph, from which the executable graph was instantiated.

{\ttfamily h\+Node} must not have been removed from the original graph.

The modifications only affect future launches of {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec}. Already enqueued or running launches of {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec} are not affected by this call. {\ttfamily h\+Node} is also not modified by this call.

Changing {\ttfamily node\+Params-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}num\+Ext\+Sems} is not supported.

\index{cuGraphExecHostNodeSetParams@{cuGraphExecHostNodeSetParams}!Graph Management@{Graph Management}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuGraphExecHostNodeSetParams()}{cuGraphExecHostNodeSetParams()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Graph\+Exec\+Host\+Node\+Set\+Params (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf0abeceeaa9f0a39592fe36a538ea1f0}{CUgraph\+Exec}}}]{h\+Graph\+Exec,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gac72514a94dacc85ed0617f979211079c}{CUgraph\+Node}}}]{h\+Node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_c_u_d_a___h_o_s_t___n_o_d_e___p_a_r_a_m_s__st}{CUDA\+\_\+\+HOST\+\_\+\+NODE\+\_\+\+PARAMS}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{node\+Params }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Sets the parameters for a host node in the given graph\+Exec. 

Updates the work represented by {\ttfamily h\+Node} in {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec} as though {\ttfamily h\+Node} had contained {\ttfamily node\+Params} at instantiation. h\+Node must remain in the graph which was used to instantiate {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec}. Changed edges to and from h\+Node are ignored.

The modifications only affect future launches of {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec}. Already enqueued or running launches of {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec} are not affected by this call. h\+Node is also not modified by this call.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em h\+Graph\+Exec} & -\/ The executable graph in which to set the specified node \\
\hline
{\em h\+Node} & -\/ Host node from the graph which was used to instantiate graph\+Exec \\
\hline
{\em node\+Params} & -\/ The updated parameters to set\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa0eed720f8a87cd1c5fd1c453bc7a03d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+SUCCESS}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa90696c86fcee1f536a1ec7d25867feeb}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE}, \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+graph\+\_\+thread\+\_\+safety \textbackslash{}notefnerr
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuGraphExecKernelNodeSetParams()}{cuGraphExecKernelNodeSetParams()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Graph\+Exec\+Kernel\+Node\+Set\+Params (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf0abeceeaa9f0a39592fe36a538ea1f0}{CUgraph\+Exec}}}]{h\+Graph\+Exec,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gac72514a94dacc85ed0617f979211079c}{CUgraph\+Node}}}]{h\+Node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_c_u_d_a___k_e_r_n_e_l___n_o_d_e___p_a_r_a_m_s__st}{CUDA\+\_\+\+KERNEL\+\_\+\+NODE\+\_\+\+PARAMS}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{node\+Params }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Sets the parameters for a kernel node in the given graph\+Exec. 

Sets the parameters of a kernel node in an executable graph {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec}. The node is identified by the corresponding node {\ttfamily h\+Node} in the non-\/executable graph, from which the executable graph was instantiated.

{\ttfamily h\+Node} must not have been removed from the original graph. All {\ttfamily node\+Params} fields may change, but the following restrictions apply to {\ttfamily func} updates\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The owning context of the function cannot change.
\item A node whose function originally did not use CUDA dynamic parallelism cannot be updated to a function which uses CDP
\end{DoxyItemize}

The modifications only affect future launches of {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec}. Already enqueued or running launches of {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec} are not affected by this call. {\ttfamily h\+Node} is also not modified by this call.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em h\+Graph\+Exec} & -\/ The executable graph in which to set the specified node \\
\hline
{\em h\+Node} & -\/ kernel node from the graph from which graph\+Exec was instantiated \\
\hline
{\em node\+Params} & -\/ Updated Parameters to set\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa0eed720f8a87cd1c5fd1c453bc7a03d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+SUCCESS}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa90696c86fcee1f536a1ec7d25867feeb}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE}, \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+graph\+\_\+thread\+\_\+safety \textbackslash{}notefnerr
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___g_r_a_p_h_gafd3e70a8c690520164fcecd02e816ab3}{cu\+Graph\+Add\+Kernel\+Node}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___g_r_a_p_h_ga4e58cd8707a87e2819afa72bf4047def}{cu\+Graph\+Kernel\+Node\+Set\+Params}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___g_r_a_p_h_ga56c8f57ab303e0029e78081d3ee122b0}{cu\+Graph\+Exec\+Memcpy\+Node\+Set\+Params}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___g_r_a_p_h_gaad747c6b429fb43f5651f7f09b26baf6}{cu\+Graph\+Exec\+Memset\+Node\+Set\+Params}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___g_r_a_p_h_ga0ab7b1f0e054b99f949baa20241cb78d}{cu\+Graph\+Exec\+Host\+Node\+Set\+Params}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___g_r_a_p_h_ga41345fc9086b2716a4044e71bb5b4db1}{cu\+Graph\+Exec\+Child\+Graph\+Node\+Set\+Params}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___g_r_a_p_h_gaf677a97a743d0976ee708444d84cc2c3}{cu\+Graph\+Exec\+Event\+Record\+Node\+Set\+Event}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___g_r_a_p_h_ga09c4d479ed40da02a5572ac7e910570a}{cu\+Graph\+Exec\+Event\+Wait\+Node\+Set\+Event}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___g_r_a_p_h_gab6d8494f141675f3a86eef225fcdbc14}{cu\+Graph\+Exec\+External\+Semaphores\+Signal\+Node\+Set\+Params}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___g_r_a_p_h_ga64160851b27b2baba2f808e208e9ee16}{cu\+Graph\+Exec\+External\+Semaphores\+Wait\+Node\+Set\+Params}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___g_r_a_p_h_gaeea2f038a4e76e7949b7c43c51848106}{cu\+Graph\+Exec\+Update}, cu\+Graph\+Instantiate

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuGraphExecMemcpyNodeSetParams()}{cuGraphExecMemcpyNodeSetParams()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Graph\+Exec\+Memcpy\+Node\+Set\+Params (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf0abeceeaa9f0a39592fe36a538ea1f0}{CUgraph\+Exec}}}]{h\+Graph\+Exec,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gac72514a94dacc85ed0617f979211079c}{CUgraph\+Node}}}]{h\+Node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_c_u_d_a___m_e_m_c_p_y3_d__st}{CUDA\+\_\+\+MEMCPY3D}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{copy\+Params,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf9f5bd81658f866613785b3a0bb7d7d9}{CUcontext}}}]{ctx }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Sets the parameters for a memcpy node in the given graph\+Exec. 

Updates the work represented by {\ttfamily h\+Node} in {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec} as though {\ttfamily h\+Node} had contained {\ttfamily copy\+Params} at instantiation. h\+Node must remain in the graph which was used to instantiate {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec}. Changed edges to and from h\+Node are ignored.

The source and destination memory in {\ttfamily copy\+Params} must be allocated from the same contexts as the original source and destination memory. Both the instantiation-\/time memory operands and the memory operands in {\ttfamily copy\+Params} must be 1-\/dimensional. Zero-\/length operations are not supported.

The modifications only affect future launches of {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec}. Already enqueued or running launches of {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec} are not affected by this call. h\+Node is also not modified by this call.

Returns CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE if the memory operands\textquotesingle{} mappings changed or either the original or new memory operands are multidimensional.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em h\+Graph\+Exec} & -\/ The executable graph in which to set the specified node \\
\hline
{\em h\+Node} & -\/ Memcpy node from the graph which was used to instantiate graph\+Exec \\
\hline
{\em copy\+Params} & -\/ The updated parameters to set \\
\hline
{\em ctx} & -\/ Context on which to run the node\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa0eed720f8a87cd1c5fd1c453bc7a03d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+SUCCESS}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa90696c86fcee1f536a1ec7d25867feeb}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE}, \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+graph\+\_\+thread\+\_\+safety \textbackslash{}notefnerr
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuGraphExecMemsetNodeSetParams()}{cuGraphExecMemsetNodeSetParams()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Graph\+Exec\+Memset\+Node\+Set\+Params (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf0abeceeaa9f0a39592fe36a538ea1f0}{CUgraph\+Exec}}}]{h\+Graph\+Exec,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gac72514a94dacc85ed0617f979211079c}{CUgraph\+Node}}}]{h\+Node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_c_u_d_a___m_e_m_s_e_t___n_o_d_e___p_a_r_a_m_s__st}{CUDA\+\_\+\+MEMSET\+\_\+\+NODE\+\_\+\+PARAMS}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{memset\+Params,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf9f5bd81658f866613785b3a0bb7d7d9}{CUcontext}}}]{ctx }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Sets the parameters for a memset node in the given graph\+Exec. 

Updates the work represented by {\ttfamily h\+Node} in {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec} as though {\ttfamily h\+Node} had contained {\ttfamily memset\+Params} at instantiation. h\+Node must remain in the graph which was used to instantiate {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec}. Changed edges to and from h\+Node are ignored.

The destination memory in {\ttfamily memset\+Params} must be allocated from the same contexts as the original destination memory. Both the instantiation-\/time memory operand and the memory operand in {\ttfamily memset\+Params} must be 1-\/dimensional. Zero-\/length operations are not supported.

The modifications only affect future launches of {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec}. Already enqueued or running launches of {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec} are not affected by this call. h\+Node is also not modified by this call.

Returns CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE if the memory operand\textquotesingle{}s mappings changed or either the original or new memory operand are multidimensional.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em h\+Graph\+Exec} & -\/ The executable graph in which to set the specified node \\
\hline
{\em h\+Node} & -\/ Memset node from the graph which was used to instantiate graph\+Exec \\
\hline
{\em memset\+Params} & -\/ The updated parameters to set \\
\hline
{\em ctx} & -\/ Context on which to run the node\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___g_r_a_p_h_ga1f8d97f9ea33996202dca1c54e5fa303}{cu\+Graph\+Add\+Memset\+Node}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___g_r_a_p_h_ga5021a01bc59279b87b1202ba80ad8f9c}{cu\+Graph\+Memset\+Node\+Set\+Params}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___g_r_a_p_h_gaa898f6157c4c6fb664cd85092fec5c0c}{cu\+Graph\+Exec\+Kernel\+Node\+Set\+Params}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___g_r_a_p_h_ga56c8f57ab303e0029e78081d3ee122b0}{cu\+Graph\+Exec\+Memcpy\+Node\+Set\+Params}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___g_r_a_p_h_ga0ab7b1f0e054b99f949baa20241cb78d}{cu\+Graph\+Exec\+Host\+Node\+Set\+Params}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___g_r_a_p_h_ga41345fc9086b2716a4044e71bb5b4db1}{cu\+Graph\+Exec\+Child\+Graph\+Node\+Set\+Params}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___g_r_a_p_h_gaf677a97a743d0976ee708444d84cc2c3}{cu\+Graph\+Exec\+Event\+Record\+Node\+Set\+Event}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___g_r_a_p_h_ga09c4d479ed40da02a5572ac7e910570a}{cu\+Graph\+Exec\+Event\+Wait\+Node\+Set\+Event}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___g_r_a_p_h_gab6d8494f141675f3a86eef225fcdbc14}{cu\+Graph\+Exec\+External\+Semaphores\+Signal\+Node\+Set\+Params}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___g_r_a_p_h_ga64160851b27b2baba2f808e208e9ee16}{cu\+Graph\+Exec\+External\+Semaphores\+Wait\+Node\+Set\+Params}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___g_r_a_p_h_gaeea2f038a4e76e7949b7c43c51848106}{cu\+Graph\+Exec\+Update}, cu\+Graph\+Instantiate

\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a___g_r_a_p_h_gaeea2f038a4e76e7949b7c43c51848106}\label{group___c_u_d_a___g_r_a_p_h_gaeea2f038a4e76e7949b7c43c51848106} 
\index{Graph Management@{Graph Management}!cuGraphExecUpdate@{cuGraphExecUpdate}}
\index{cuGraphExecUpdate@{cuGraphExecUpdate}!Graph Management@{Graph Management}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuGraphExecUpdate()}{cuGraphExecUpdate()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Graph\+Exec\+Update (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf0abeceeaa9f0a39592fe36a538ea1f0}{CUgraph\+Exec}}}]{h\+Graph\+Exec,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga69f555c38df5b3fa1ed25efef794739a}{CUgraph}}}]{h\+Graph,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gac72514a94dacc85ed0617f979211079c}{CUgraph\+Node}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{h\+Error\+Node\+\_\+out,  }\item[{CUgraph\+Exec\+Update\+Result \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{update\+Result\+\_\+out }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Check whether an executable graph can be updated with a graph and perform the update if possible. 

Updates the node parameters in the instantiated graph specified by {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec} with the node parameters in a topologically identical graph specified by {\ttfamily h\+Graph}.

Limitations\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Kernel nodes\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The owning context of the function cannot change.
\item A node whose function originally did not use CUDA dynamic parallelism cannot be updated to a function which uses CDP.
\item A cooperative node cannot be updated to a non-\/cooperative node, and vice-\/versa.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Memset and memcpy nodes\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The CUDA device(s) to which the operand(s) was allocated/mapped cannot change.
\item The source/destination memory must be allocated from the same contexts as the original source/destination memory.
\item Only 1D memsets can be changed.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Additional memcpy node restrictions\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Changing either the source or destination memory type(i.\+e. CU\+\_\+\+MEMORYTYPE\+\_\+\+DEVICE, CU\+\_\+\+MEMORYTYPE\+\_\+\+ARRAY, etc.) is not supported.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item External semaphore wait nodes and record nodes\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Changing the number of semaphores is not supported.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}

Note\+: The API may add further restrictions in future releases. The return code should always be checked.

cu\+Graph\+Exec\+Update sets {\ttfamily update\+Result\+\_\+out} to CU\+\_\+\+GRAPH\+\_\+\+EXEC\+\_\+\+UPDATE\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+TOPOLOGY\+\_\+\+CHANGED under the following conditions\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The count of nodes directly in {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec} and {\ttfamily h\+Graph} differ, in which case {\ttfamily h\+Error\+Node\+\_\+out} is NULL.
\item A node is deleted in {\ttfamily h\+Graph} but not not its pair from {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec}, in which case {\ttfamily h\+Error\+Node\+\_\+out} is NULL.
\item A node is deleted in {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec} but not its pair from {\ttfamily h\+Graph}, in which case {\ttfamily h\+Error\+Node\+\_\+out} is the pairless node from {\ttfamily h\+Graph}.
\item The dependent nodes of a pair differ, in which case {\ttfamily h\+Error\+Node\+\_\+out} is the node from {\ttfamily h\+Graph}.
\end{DoxyItemize}

cu\+Graph\+Exec\+Update sets {\ttfamily update\+Result\+\_\+out} to\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item CU\+\_\+\+GRAPH\+\_\+\+EXEC\+\_\+\+UPDATE\+\_\+\+ERROR if passed an invalid value.
\item CU\+\_\+\+GRAPH\+\_\+\+EXEC\+\_\+\+UPDATE\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+TOPOLOGY\+\_\+\+CHANGED if the graph topology changed
\item CU\+\_\+\+GRAPH\+\_\+\+EXEC\+\_\+\+UPDATE\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+NODE\+\_\+\+TYPE\+\_\+\+CHANGED if the type of a node changed, in which case {\ttfamily h\+Error\+Node\+\_\+out} is set to the node from {\ttfamily h\+Graph}.
\item CU\+\_\+\+GRAPH\+\_\+\+EXEC\+\_\+\+UPDATE\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+UNSUPPORTED\+\_\+\+FUNCTION\+\_\+\+CHANGE if the function changed in an unsupported way(see note above), in which case {\ttfamily h\+Error\+Node\+\_\+out} is set to the node from {\ttfamily h\+Graph} 
\item CU\+\_\+\+GRAPH\+\_\+\+EXEC\+\_\+\+UPDATE\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+PARAMETERS\+\_\+\+CHANGED if any parameters to a node changed in a way that is not supported, in which case {\ttfamily h\+Error\+Node\+\_\+out} is set to the node from {\ttfamily h\+Graph}.
\item CU\+\_\+\+GRAPH\+\_\+\+EXEC\+\_\+\+UPDATE\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+ATTRIBUTES\+\_\+\+CHANGED if any attributes of a node changed in a way that is not supported, in which case {\ttfamily h\+Error\+Node\+\_\+out} is set to the node from {\ttfamily h\+Graph}.
\item CU\+\_\+\+GRAPH\+\_\+\+EXEC\+\_\+\+UPDATE\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+SUPPORTED if something about a node is unsupported, like the node\textquotesingle{}s type or configuration, in which case {\ttfamily h\+Error\+Node\+\_\+out} is set to the node from {\ttfamily h\+Graph} 
\end{DoxyItemize}

If {\ttfamily update\+Result\+\_\+out} isn\textquotesingle{}t set in one of the situations described above, the update check passes and cu\+Graph\+Exec\+Update updates {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec} to match the contents of {\ttfamily h\+Graph}. If an error happens during the update, {\ttfamily update\+Result\+\_\+out} will be set to CU\+\_\+\+GRAPH\+\_\+\+EXEC\+\_\+\+UPDATE\+\_\+\+ERROR; otherwise, {\ttfamily update\+Result\+\_\+out} is set to CU\+\_\+\+GRAPH\+\_\+\+EXEC\+\_\+\+UPDATE\+\_\+\+SUCCESS.

cu\+Graph\+Exec\+Update returns CUDA\+\_\+\+SUCCESS when the updated was performed successfully. It returns CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+GRAPH\+\_\+\+EXEC\+\_\+\+UPDATE\+\_\+\+FAILURE if the graph update was not performed because it included changes which violated constraints specific to instantiated graph update.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em h\+Graph\+Exec} & The instantiated graph to be updated \\
\hline
{\em h\+Graph} & The graph containing the updated parameters \\
\hline
{\em h\+Error\+Node\+\_\+out} & The node which caused the permissibility check to forbid the update, if any \\
\hline
{\em update\+Result\+\_\+out} & Whether the graph update was permitted. If was forbidden, the reason why\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa0eed720f8a87cd1c5fd1c453bc7a03d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+SUCCESS}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa114e389888b89d68639b330f478386c6}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+GRAPH\+\_\+\+EXEC\+\_\+\+UPDATE\+\_\+\+FAILURE}, \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+graph\+\_\+thread\+\_\+safety \textbackslash{}notefnerr
\end{DoxyReturn}

Returns an external semaphore signal node\textquotesingle{}s parameters. 

Returns the parameters of an external semaphore signal node {\ttfamily h\+Node} in {\ttfamily params\+\_\+out}. The {\ttfamily ext\+Sem\+Array} and {\ttfamily params\+Array} returned in {\ttfamily params\+\_\+out}, are owned by the node. This memory remains valid until the node is destroyed or its parameters are modified, and should not be modified directly. Use \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___g_r_a_p_h_ga5cb92de7ad85a5c2e847441570b6e566}{cu\+Graph\+External\+Semaphores\+Signal\+Node\+Set\+Params} to update the parameters of this node.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuGraphGetEdges()}{cuGraphGetEdges()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Graph\+Get\+Edges (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga69f555c38df5b3fa1ed25efef794739a}{CUgraph}}}]{h\+Graph,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gac72514a94dacc85ed0617f979211079c}{CUgraph\+Node}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{from,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gac72514a94dacc85ed0617f979211079c}{CUgraph\+Node}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{to,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{num\+Edges }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Returns a graph\textquotesingle{}s dependency edges. 

Returns a list of {\ttfamily h\+Graph\textquotesingle{}s} dependency edges. Edges are returned via corresponding indices in {\ttfamily from} and {\ttfamily to}; that is, the node in {\ttfamily to}\mbox{[}i\mbox{]} has a dependency on the node in {\ttfamily from}\mbox{[}i\mbox{]}. {\ttfamily from} and {\ttfamily to} may both be NULL, in which case this function only returns the number of edges in {\ttfamily num\+Edges}. Otherwise, {\ttfamily num\+Edges} entries will be filled in. If {\ttfamily num\+Edges} is higher than the actual number of edges, the remaining entries in {\ttfamily from} and {\ttfamily to} will be set to NULL, and the number of edges actually returned will be written to {\ttfamily num\+Edges}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em h\+Graph} & -\/ Graph to get the edges from \\
\hline
{\em from} & -\/ Location to return edge endpoints \\
\hline
{\em to} & -\/ Location to return edge endpoints \\
\hline
{\em num\+Edges} & -\/ See description\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa0eed720f8a87cd1c5fd1c453bc7a03d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+SUCCESS}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaacf52f132faf29b473cdda6061f0f44a}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+DEINITIALIZED}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa8feb999f0af99b4a25ab26b3866f4df8}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa90696c86fcee1f536a1ec7d25867feeb}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE} \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+graph\+\_\+thread\+\_\+safety \textbackslash{}notefnerr
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuGraphGetNodes()}{cuGraphGetNodes()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Graph\+Get\+Nodes (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga69f555c38df5b3fa1ed25efef794739a}{CUgraph}}}]{h\+Graph,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gac72514a94dacc85ed0617f979211079c}{CUgraph\+Node}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{nodes,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{num\+Nodes }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Returns a graph\textquotesingle{}s nodes. 

Returns a list of {\ttfamily h\+Graph\textquotesingle{}s} nodes. {\ttfamily nodes} may be NULL, in which case this function will return the number of nodes in {\ttfamily num\+Nodes}. Otherwise, {\ttfamily num\+Nodes} entries will be filled in. If {\ttfamily num\+Nodes} is higher than the actual number of nodes, the remaining entries in {\ttfamily nodes} will be set to NULL, and the number of nodes actually obtained will be returned in {\ttfamily num\+Nodes}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em h\+Graph} & -\/ Graph to query \\
\hline
{\em nodes} & -\/ Pointer to return the nodes \\
\hline
{\em num\+Nodes} & -\/ See description\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
