\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuGraphInstantiate()}{cuGraphInstantiate()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Graph\+Instantiate (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf0abeceeaa9f0a39592fe36a538ea1f0}{CUgraph\+Exec}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{ph\+Graph\+Exec,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga69f555c38df5b3fa1ed25efef794739a}{CUgraph}}}]{h\+Graph,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gac72514a94dacc85ed0617f979211079c}{CUgraph\+Node}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{ph\+Error\+Node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{char}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{log\+Buffer,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{buffer\+Size }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Creates an executable graph from a graph. 

Instantiates {\ttfamily h\+Graph} as an executable graph. The graph is validated for any structural constraints or intra-\/node constraints which were not previously validated. If instantiation is successful, a handle to the instantiated graph is returned in {\ttfamily ph\+Graph\+Exec}.

If there are any errors, diagnostic information may be returned in {\ttfamily error\+Node} and {\ttfamily log\+Buffer}. This is the primary way to inspect instantiation errors. The output will be null terminated unless the diagnostics overflow the buffer. In this case, they will be truncated, and the last byte can be inspected to determine if truncation occurred.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ph\+Graph\+Exec} & -\/ Returns instantiated graph \\
\hline
{\em h\+Graph} & -\/ Graph to instantiate \\
\hline
{\em ph\+Error\+Node} & -\/ In case of an instantiation error, this may be modified to indicate a node contributing to the error \\
\hline
{\em log\+Buffer} & -\/ A character buffer to store diagnostic messages \\
\hline
{\em buffer\+Size} & -\/ Size of the log buffer in bytes\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa0eed720f8a87cd1c5fd1c453bc7a03d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+SUCCESS}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaacf52f132faf29b473cdda6061f0f44a}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+DEINITIALIZED}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa8feb999f0af99b4a25ab26b3866f4df8}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa90696c86fcee1f536a1ec7d25867feeb}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE} \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+graph\+\_\+thread\+\_\+safety \textbackslash{}notefnerr
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___g_r_a_p_h_gab6fd709bfe08bd3304c53d9924039fc8}{cu\+Graph\+Instantiate\+With\+Flags}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___g_r_a_p_h_gae28b0ab067d331b5ed7efc9e318b2ccd}{cu\+Graph\+Create}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___g_r_a_p_h_ga788cf6ef7e02a509fbba33fde9b7a6da}{cu\+Graph\+Upload}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___g_r_a_p_h_ga6da62b37e203741ab40b2474331e6c49}{cu\+Graph\+Launch}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___g_r_a_p_h_gaaf662c6e239c843da8865590734df893}{cu\+Graph\+Exec\+Destroy} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a___g_r_a_p_h_gab6fd709bfe08bd3304c53d9924039fc8}\label{group___c_u_d_a___g_r_a_p_h_gab6fd709bfe08bd3304c53d9924039fc8} 
\index{Graph Management@{Graph Management}!cuGraphInstantiateWithFlags@{cuGraphInstantiateWithFlags}}
\index{cuGraphInstantiateWithFlags@{cuGraphInstantiateWithFlags}!Graph Management@{Graph Management}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuGraphInstantiateWithFlags()}{cuGraphInstantiateWithFlags()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Graph\+Instantiate\+With\+Flags (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf0abeceeaa9f0a39592fe36a538ea1f0}{CUgraph\+Exec}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{ph\+Graph\+Exec,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga69f555c38df5b3fa1ed25efef794739a}{CUgraph}}}]{h\+Graph,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{unsigned}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{long}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{long}}}]{flags }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Creates an executable graph from a graph. 

Instantiates {\ttfamily h\+Graph} as an executable graph. The graph is validated for any structural constraints or intra-\/node constraints which were not previously validated. If instantiation is successful, a handle to the instantiated graph is returned in {\ttfamily ph\+Graph\+Exec}.

The {\ttfamily flags} parameter controls the behavior of instantiation and subsequent graph launches. Valid flags are\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggac3b9348f257350775565dd26cc4ce6e3a1684f715bf05e39afd69aa508299a479}{CUDA\+\_\+\+GRAPH\+\_\+\+INSTANTIATE\+\_\+\+FLAG\+\_\+\+AUTO\+\_\+\+FREE\+\_\+\+ON\+\_\+\+LAUNCH}, which configures a graph containing memory allocation nodes to automatically free any unfreed memory allocations before the graph is relaunched.
\end{DoxyItemize}

If {\ttfamily h\+Graph} contains any allocation or free nodes, there can be at most one executable graph in existence for that graph at a time.

An attempt to instantiate a second executable graph before destroying the first with \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___g_r_a_p_h_gaaf662c6e239c843da8865590734df893}{cu\+Graph\+Exec\+Destroy} will result in an error.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ph\+Graph\+Exec} & -\/ Returns instantiated graph \\
\hline
{\em h\+Graph} & -\/ Graph to instantiate \\
\hline
{\em flags} & -\/ Flags to control instantiation. See \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gabc4dc810c9913d836bf62a7b2be791dd}{CUgraph\+Instantiate\+\_\+flags}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuGraphKernelNodeGetParams()}{cuGraphKernelNodeGetParams()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Graph\+Kernel\+Node\+Get\+Params (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gac72514a94dacc85ed0617f979211079c}{CUgraph\+Node}}}]{h\+Node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_c_u_d_a___k_e_r_n_e_l___n_o_d_e___p_a_r_a_m_s__st}{CUDA\+\_\+\+KERNEL\+\_\+\+NODE\+\_\+\+PARAMS}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{node\+Params }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Returns a kernel node\textquotesingle{}s parameters. 

Returns the parameters of kernel node {\ttfamily h\+Node} in {\ttfamily node\+Params}. The {\ttfamily kernel\+Params} or {\ttfamily extra} array returned in {\ttfamily node\+Params}, as well as the argument values it points to, are owned by the node. This memory remains valid until the node is destroyed or its parameters are modified, and should not be modified directly. Use \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___g_r_a_p_h_ga4e58cd8707a87e2819afa72bf4047def}{cu\+Graph\+Kernel\+Node\+Set\+Params} to update the parameters of this node.

The params will contain either {\ttfamily kernel\+Params} or {\ttfamily extra}, according to which of these was most recently set on the node.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em h\+Node} & -\/ Node to get the parameters for \\
\hline
{\em node\+Params} & -\/ Pointer to return the parameters\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuGraphLaunch()}{cuGraphLaunch()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Graph\+Launch (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf0abeceeaa9f0a39592fe36a538ea1f0}{CUgraph\+Exec}}}]{h\+Graph\+Exec,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gab946c7f02e09efd788a204718015d88a}{CUstream}}}]{h\+Stream }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Launches an executable graph in a stream. 

Executes {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec} in {\ttfamily h\+Stream}. Only one instance of {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec} may be executing at a time. Each launch is ordered behind both any previous work in {\ttfamily h\+Stream} and any previous launches of {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec}. To execute a graph concurrently, it must be instantiated multiple times into multiple executable graphs.

If any allocations created by {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec} remain unfreed (from a previous launch) and {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec} was not instantiated with \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggac3b9348f257350775565dd26cc4ce6e3a1684f715bf05e39afd69aa508299a479}{CUDA\+\_\+\+GRAPH\+\_\+\+INSTANTIATE\+\_\+\+FLAG\+\_\+\+AUTO\+\_\+\+FREE\+\_\+\+ON\+\_\+\+LAUNCH}, the launch will fail with \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa90696c86fcee1f536a1ec7d25867feeb}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em h\+Graph\+Exec} & -\/ Executable graph to launch \\
\hline
{\em h\+Stream} & -\/ Stream in which to launch the graph\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa0eed720f8a87cd1c5fd1c453bc7a03d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+SUCCESS}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaacf52f132faf29b473cdda6061f0f44a}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+DEINITIALIZED}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa8feb999f0af99b4a25ab26b3866f4df8}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa90696c86fcee1f536a1ec7d25867feeb}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE} \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+graph\+\_\+thread\+\_\+safety \textbackslash{}notefnerr
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Graph\+Mem\+Alloc\+Node\+Get\+Params (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gac72514a94dacc85ed0617f979211079c}{CUgraph\+Node}}}]{h\+Node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gac27ce5ce8b444b2120a2a27712d93681}{CUDA\+\_\+\+MEM\+\_\+\+ALLOC\+\_\+\+NODE\+\_\+\+PARAMS}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{params\+\_\+out }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Returns a memory alloc node\textquotesingle{}s parameters. 

Returns the parameters of a memory alloc node {\ttfamily h\+Node} in {\ttfamily params\+\_\+out}. The {\ttfamily pool\+Props} and {\ttfamily access\+Descs} returned in {\ttfamily params\+\_\+out}, are owned by the node. This memory remains valid until the node is destroyed. The returned parameters must not be modified.

\index{Graph Management@{Graph Management}!cuGraphNodeFindInClone@{cuGraphNodeFindInClone}}
\index{cuGraphNodeFindInClone@{cuGraphNodeFindInClone}!Graph Management@{Graph Management}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuGraphNodeFindInClone()}{cuGraphNodeFindInClone()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Graph\+Node\+Find\+In\+Clone (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gac72514a94dacc85ed0617f979211079c}{CUgraph\+Node}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{ph\+Node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gac72514a94dacc85ed0617f979211079c}{CUgraph\+Node}}}]{h\+Original\+Node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga69f555c38df5b3fa1ed25efef794739a}{CUgraph}}}]{h\+Cloned\+Graph }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Finds a cloned version of a node. 

This function returns the node in {\ttfamily h\+Cloned\+Graph} corresponding to {\ttfamily h\+Original\+Node} in the original graph.

{\ttfamily h\+Cloned\+Graph} must have been cloned from {\ttfamily h\+Original\+Graph} via \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___g_r_a_p_h_ga5a4f3ffa777b1b9d7ecdd9e0256e081a}{cu\+Graph\+Clone}. {\ttfamily h\+Original\+Node} must have been in {\ttfamily h\+Original\+Graph} at the time of the call to \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___g_r_a_p_h_ga5a4f3ffa777b1b9d7ecdd9e0256e081a}{cu\+Graph\+Clone}, and the corresponding cloned node in {\ttfamily h\+Cloned\+Graph} must not have been removed. The cloned node is then returned via {\ttfamily ph\+Cloned\+Node}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ph\+Node} & -\/ Returns handle to the cloned node \\
\hline
{\em h\+Original\+Node} & -\/ Handle to the original node \\
\hline
{\em h\+Cloned\+Graph} & -\/ Cloned graph to query\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa0eed720f8a87cd1c5fd1c453bc7a03d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+SUCCESS}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa90696c86fcee1f536a1ec7d25867feeb}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE}, \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+graph\+\_\+thread\+\_\+safety \textbackslash{}notefnerr
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuGraphNodeGetDependencies()}{cuGraphNodeGetDependencies()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Graph\+Node\+Get\+Dependencies (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gac72514a94dacc85ed0617f979211079c}{CUgraph\+Node}}}]{h\+Node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gac72514a94dacc85ed0617f979211079c}{CUgraph\+Node}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dependencies,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{num\+Dependencies }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Returns a node\textquotesingle{}s dependencies. 

Returns a list of {\ttfamily node\textquotesingle{}s} dependencies. {\ttfamily dependencies} may be NULL, in which case this function will return the number of dependencies in {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies}. Otherwise, {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} entries will be filled in. If {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} is higher than the actual number of dependencies, the remaining entries in {\ttfamily dependencies} will be set to NULL, and the number of nodes actually obtained will be returned in {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em h\+Node} & -\/ Node to query \\
\hline
{\em dependencies} & -\/ Pointer to return the dependencies \\
\hline
{\em num\+Dependencies} & -\/ See description\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa0eed720f8a87cd1c5fd1c453bc7a03d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+SUCCESS}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaacf52f132faf29b473cdda6061f0f44a}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+DEINITIALIZED}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa8feb999f0af99b4a25ab26b3866f4df8}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa90696c86fcee1f536a1ec7d25867feeb}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE} \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+graph\+\_\+thread\+\_\+safety \textbackslash{}notefnerr
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Graph\+Node\+Get\+Dependent\+Nodes (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gac72514a94dacc85ed0617f979211079c}{CUgraph\+Node}}}]{h\+Node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gac72514a94dacc85ed0617f979211079c}{CUgraph\+Node}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dependent\+Nodes,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{num\+Dependent\+Nodes }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Returns a node\textquotesingle{}s dependent nodes. 

Returns a list of {\ttfamily node\textquotesingle{}s} dependent nodes. {\ttfamily dependent\+Nodes} may be NULL, in which case this function will return the number of dependent nodes in {\ttfamily num\+Dependent\+Nodes}. Otherwise, {\ttfamily num\+Dependent\+Nodes} entries will be filled in. If {\ttfamily num\+Dependent\+Nodes} is higher than the actual number of dependent nodes, the remaining entries in {\ttfamily dependent\+Nodes} will be set to NULL, and the number of nodes actually obtained will be returned in {\ttfamily num\+Dependent\+Nodes}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em h\+Node} & -\/ Node to query \\
\hline
{\em dependent\+Nodes} & -\/ Pointer to return the dependent nodes \\
\hline
{\em num\+Dependent\+Nodes} & -\/ See description\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuGraphNodeGetEnabled()}{cuGraphNodeGetEnabled()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Graph\+Node\+Get\+Enabled (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf0abeceeaa9f0a39592fe36a538ea1f0}{CUgraph\+Exec}}}]{h\+Graph\+Exec,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gac72514a94dacc85ed0617f979211079c}{CUgraph\+Node}}}]{h\+Node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{unsigned}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{int}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{is\+Enabled }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Query whether a node in the given graph\+Exec is enabled. 

Sets is\+Enabled to 1 if {\ttfamily h\+Node} is enabled, or 0 if {\ttfamily h\+Node} is disabled.

The node is identified by the corresponding node {\ttfamily h\+Node} in the non-\/executable graph, from which the executable graph was instantiated. ~\newline


{\ttfamily h\+Node} must not have been removed from the original graph.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Currently only kernel nodes are supported.
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em h\+Graph\+Exec} & -\/ The executable graph in which to set the specified node \\
\hline
{\em h\+Node} & -\/ Node from the graph from which graph\+Exec was instantiated \\
\hline
{\em is\+Enabled} & -\/ Location to return the enabled status of the node\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\index{Graph Management@{Graph Management}!cuGraphNodeSetEnabled@{cuGraphNodeSetEnabled}}
\index{cuGraphNodeSetEnabled@{cuGraphNodeSetEnabled}!Graph Management@{Graph Management}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuGraphNodeSetEnabled()}{cuGraphNodeSetEnabled()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Graph\+Node\+Set\+Enabled (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf0abeceeaa9f0a39592fe36a538ea1f0}{CUgraph\+Exec}}}]{h\+Graph\+Exec,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gac72514a94dacc85ed0617f979211079c}{CUgraph\+Node}}}]{h\+Node,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{unsigned}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{int}}}]{is\+Enabled }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Enables or disables the specified node in the given graph\+Exec. 

Sets {\ttfamily h\+Node} to be either enabled or disabled. Disabled nodes are functionally equivalent to empty nodes until they are reenabled. Existing node parameters are not affected by disabling/enabling the node.

The node is identified by the corresponding node {\ttfamily h\+Node} in the non-\/executable graph, from which the executable graph was instantiated. ~\newline


{\ttfamily h\+Node} must not have been removed from the original graph.

The modifications only affect future launches of {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec}. Already enqueued or running launches of {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec} are not affected by this call. {\ttfamily h\+Node} is also not modified by this call.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Currently only kernel nodes are supported.
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em h\+Graph\+Exec} & -\/ The executable graph in which to set the specified node \\
\hline
{\em h\+Node} & -\/ Node from the graph from which graph\+Exec was instantiated \\
\hline
{\em is\+Enabled} & -\/ Node is enabled if != 0, otherwise the node is disabled\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa0eed720f8a87cd1c5fd1c453bc7a03d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+SUCCESS}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa90696c86fcee1f536a1ec7d25867feeb}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE}, \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+graph\+\_\+thread\+\_\+safety \textbackslash{}notefnerr
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuGraphRemoveDependencies()}{cuGraphRemoveDependencies()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Graph\+Remove\+Dependencies (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga69f555c38df5b3fa1ed25efef794739a}{CUgraph}}}]{h\+Graph,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gac72514a94dacc85ed0617f979211079c}{CUgraph\+Node}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{from,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gac72514a94dacc85ed0617f979211079c}{CUgraph\+Node}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{to,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{num\+Dependencies }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Removes dependency edges from a graph. 

The number of {\ttfamily dependencies} to be removed is defined by {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies}. Elements in {\ttfamily from} and {\ttfamily to} at corresponding indices define a dependency. Each node in {\ttfamily from} and {\ttfamily to} must belong to {\ttfamily h\+Graph}.

If {\ttfamily num\+Dependencies} is 0, elements in {\ttfamily from} and {\ttfamily to} will be ignored. Specifying a non-\/existing dependency will return an error.

Dependencies cannot be removed from graphs which contain allocation or free nodes. Any attempt to do so will return an error.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em h\+Graph} & -\/ Graph from which to remove dependencies \\
\hline
{\em from} & -\/ Array of nodes that provide the dependencies \\
\hline
{\em to} & -\/ Array of dependent nodes \\
\hline
{\em num\+Dependencies} & -\/ Number of dependencies to be removed\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa0eed720f8a87cd1c5fd1c453bc7a03d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+SUCCESS}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa90696c86fcee1f536a1ec7d25867feeb}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE} \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+graph\+\_\+thread\+\_\+safety \textbackslash{}notefnerr
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuGraphRetainUserObject()}{cuGraphRetainUserObject()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Graph\+Retain\+User\+Object (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga69f555c38df5b3fa1ed25efef794739a}{CUgraph}}}]{graph,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga2578b65c87dc98d336f99edca913e92b}{CUuser\+Object}}}]{object,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{unsigned}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{int}}}]{count,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{unsigned}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{int}}}]{flags }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Retain a reference to a user object from a graph. 

Creates or moves user object references that will be owned by a CUDA graph.

See CUDA User Objects in the CUDA C++ Programming Guide for more information on user objects.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em graph} & -\/ The graph to associate the reference with \\
\hline
{\em object} & -\/ The user object to retain a reference for \\
\hline
{\em count} & -\/ The number of references to add to the graph, typically 1. Must be nonzero and not larger than INT\+\_\+\+MAX. \\
\hline
{\em flags} & -\/ The optional flag \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggacdb8e9f9eed14003445854d5cad7b5bcaf9b815bff431e87e54037568c4677b9d}{CU\+\_\+\+GRAPH\+\_\+\+USER\+\_\+\+OBJECT\+\_\+\+MOVE} transfers references from the calling thread, rather than create new references. Pass 0 to create new references.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa0eed720f8a87cd1c5fd1c453bc7a03d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+SUCCESS}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa90696c86fcee1f536a1ec7d25867feeb}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE}
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuGraphUpload()}{cuGraphUpload()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Graph\+Upload (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf0abeceeaa9f0a39592fe36a538ea1f0}{CUgraph\+Exec}}}]{h\+Graph\+Exec,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gab946c7f02e09efd788a204718015d88a}{CUstream}}}]{h\+Stream }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Uploads an executable graph in a stream. 

Uploads {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec} to the device in {\ttfamily h\+Stream} without executing it. Uploads of the same {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec} will be serialized. Each upload is ordered behind both any previous work in {\ttfamily h\+Stream} and any previous launches of {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec}. Uses memory cached by {\ttfamily stream} to back the allocations owned by {\ttfamily h\+Graph\+Exec}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em h\+Graph\+Exec} & -\/ Executable graph to upload \\
\hline
{\em h\+Stream} & -\/ Stream in which to upload the graph\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa0eed720f8a87cd1c5fd1c453bc7a03d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+SUCCESS}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaacf52f132faf29b473cdda6061f0f44a}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+DEINITIALIZED}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa8feb999f0af99b4a25ab26b3866f4df8}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa90696c86fcee1f536a1ec7d25867feeb}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE} \textbackslash{}note\+\_\+graph\+\_\+thread\+\_\+safety \textbackslash{}notefnerr

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuUserObjectCreate()}{cuUserObjectCreate()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+User\+Object\+Create (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga2578b65c87dc98d336f99edca913e92b}{CUuser\+Object}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{object\+\_\+out,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{ptr,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga9acbe203a81685fde68ad76f3e94896e}{CUhost\+Fn}}}]{destroy,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{unsigned}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{int}}}]{initial\+Refcount,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{unsigned}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{int}}}]{flags }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Create a user object. 

Create a user object with the specified destructor callback and initial reference count. The initial references are owned by the caller.

Destructor callbacks cannot make CUDA API calls and should avoid blocking behavior, as they are executed by a shared internal thread. Another thread may be signaled to perform such actions, if it does not block forward progress of tasks scheduled through CUDA.

See CUDA User Objects in the CUDA C++ Programming Guide for more information on user objects.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em object\+\_\+out} & -\/ Location to return the user object handle \\
\hline
{\em ptr} & -\/ The pointer to pass to the destroy function \\
\hline
{\em destroy} & -\/ Callback to free the user object when it is no longer in use \\
\hline
{\em initial\+Refcount} & -\/ The initial refcount to create the object with, typically 1. The initial references are owned by the calling thread. \\
\hline
{\em flags} & -\/ Currently it is required to pass \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga94489b8dbd6ef66efe8cc6326fe7f5caa30bb85019bed1f36b8130cef76085e27}{CU\+\_\+\+USER\+\_\+\+OBJECT\+\_\+\+NO\+\_\+\+DESTRUCTOR\+\_\+\+SYNC}, which is the only defined flag. This indicates that the destroy callback cannot be waited on by any CUDA API. Users requiring synchronization of the callback should signal its completion manually.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa0eed720f8a87cd1c5fd1c453bc7a03d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+SUCCESS}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa90696c86fcee1f536a1ec7d25867feeb}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE}
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuUserObjectRelease()}{cuUserObjectRelease()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+User\+Object\+Release (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga2578b65c87dc98d336f99edca913e92b}{CUuser\+Object}}}]{object,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{unsigned}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{int}}}]{count }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Release a reference to a user object. 

Releases user object references owned by the caller. The object\textquotesingle{}s destructor is invoked if the reference count reaches zero.

It is undefined behavior to release references not owned by the caller, or to use a user object handle after all references are released.

See CUDA User Objects in the CUDA C++ Programming Guide for more information on user objects.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em object} & -\/ The object to release \\
\hline
{\em count} & -\/ The number of references to release, typically 1. Must be nonzero and not larger than INT\+\_\+\+MAX.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaa0eed720f8a87cd1c5fd1c453bc7a03d}{CUDA\+\_\+\+SUCCESS}, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa90696c86fcee1f536a1ec7d25867feeb}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE}
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+User\+Object\+Retain (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga2578b65c87dc98d336f99edca913e92b}{CUuser\+Object}}}]{object,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{unsigned}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{int}}}]{count }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Retain a reference to a user object. 

Retains new references to a user object. The new references are owned by the caller.
